name:L‚Äçe‚Äçe‚Äçd‚Äç3‚Äç3‚Äç7
info:Classical Twin Room
info:Stayed in April 2024
info:Couples
info:1 Review
rating:5
posted:Posted April 5, 2024
msg:We spent 2 nights at Sheraton hotel in Guilin. The hotel is located very centrally in walking distance to most major tourist attractions and close to Guilin railway station. The staff was very attentive and absolutely accomodating for all of our wishes making our experience very memorable. The interior design of the hotel is well thought out and gives it a simple but elegant touch. The facilities include small swimming pool which we couldn't try due to the weather situation. The gym consisted of a handful of cardio treadmills and machines for resistance training from Life Fitness with an area in the corner with dumbells and foam rollers, yoga mats. The changing room came with a sauna.
We can recommend the breakfast buffet which is a mix of Western breakfast and local specialties from Guilin.
Out of the available package options we really enjoyed the photo shoot where they provide makeup and clothes(classy/elegant and Guilin traditional) to capture the amazing moments from the trip.
----------------------------------------

posted:Posted April 1, 2024
msg:The hotel location is hard to awesom!  It's walking distance to some of the best sites in Guilin and the facilities are in very good condition.

The food for breakfast is excellent! The staff were friendly and helpful, although only a portion of the staff speaks English. There were very few Americans or English speakers during my visit.  It wasn‚Äôt an issue, just of note.

I was fortunate to have a room on the top floor facing the river and got a glimpse of a beautiful sunrise one morning. At night the musicians play by the river so it isn't the most quiet location but the view is great!

One less desirable thing was they hosted a large tour group from Hong Kong on Saturday/Sunday and the group ate early and blocked access to the buffet.  The staff was very apologetic and took care of me when I returned an hour later.

It is about a 5-minute walk from the No. 3 gate of Elephant Trunk Hill. It is very convenient to eat around. Behind it is Zhengyang Pedestrian Street. Far. Next door is Yiren Road, and Chongshan Rice Noodles Main Store is only 2 or 3 minutes away, which is very convenient. The Jinlong Village recommended by the local Didi driver is also near the Sheraton. In addition, the night tour of the two rivers and four lakes personally feels unnecessary, it is better to go directly to the Lijiang River.
The check-in was very friendly. The family happened to celebrate their birthday. The front desk said that they would instruct the restaurant to make a cake and arrange the guest room. Meimeida, the cake is small, but the taste is very good, and there are fruits in it.
Forced by the epidemic, I saw Sheraton offer a group purchase of 999 yuan / 3 nights with breakfast a long time ago. I bought it immediately. Although Sheraton accepts group guests, the service has not declined in the slightest. Although the basic rooms are small, they are clean and tidy, and there are bay windows. I have stayed in the hotel for the first time and found that there are bay windows. I am very impressed. There will be two free bottles of water in the guest room every day, but due to the hot weather, Auntie Linen said that she will put two more bottles to relieve the heat, which is really considerate!
However, Sheraton Guilin also has two shortcomings. The breakfast has not changed at all for three consecutive days, and the carbs are too high. Although the bread and cakes are really delicious, the fruits are not rich enough. Lychee, yellow skin and mango season, none of these... Guilin rice noodles mainly promote mixed noodles, and Sheraton's brine is great. Why do they mainly promote soup noodles? My friend said that it is not good to eat soup noodles. I suggested to try the mixed noodles, and everyone was full of praise.
Second, it may be a common problem with Sheratons across the country. The quilt disappears when you fall asleep... I believe that friends or hotel staff who have the same experience will understand me.
Speaking of the gym, I didn‚Äôt go to the gym, but I went to watch it before it closed on the day. The opening hours are great from 6:00 to 23:00 every day. The gym is very big and well-equipped. The swimming pool is outdoor. The water depth is 1.2 meters to 2.9 meters. I shuddered when I heard this depth.
Rory talked a lot, and the overall is still very good. It was noon when we checked out. The little brother and sister at the front desk asked if you need water~ The details are great~
